msg:The first choice hotel for traveling in Jiangyin. Although it has been open for many years, the hotel facilities are not as smart as those of new hotels, but as an old high-end chain hotel, it has complete functional facilities. The hotel belongs to the garden hotel type, with its own green lake, the highest floor is seven floors, Chinese restaurant, Western restaurant, Japanese restaurant with a variety of dining options, swimming pool, gym, bar, hotel staff service is friendly, especially the front desk Xiao Gu, Xiao Zhao and Julie gave timely communication and help when leaving the hotel because the elderly at home were not familiar with the minibar paid food and took it out by mistake. The hotel is adjacent to Huangshan Lake Park and Jiangyin Fortress Forest Park. Although the main entrance is inconvenient to walk due to municipal engineering, you can walk directly to the scenic spot from the side door.
